This is probably my new favorite Sidemen video now. I really hope they do a part 2 for this, and maybe do 4 robots and make a mini tournament for it. As for the robots, they both look really good, and I knew the match was going to go 1 of 2 ways. Either Golden Daddy winning with pure destruction, or Tenderizer winning with control. It's a lot harder to control a 2 wheel robot than a 4 wheel one. Plus Tenderizer has a defensive wedge to not only deflect the blows from the disc, it also helps in a pushing match compared to a disabled disc. Spinners are some of the most successful designs out there, but once their weapon breaks, they're just sitting ducks afterwards. Hammers are cool, however most hammer bots do not do well in robot combat. Only Terrorhurtz and Beta had the most success with hammers, and they're both built by the same team. And sometimes the best defence is the best offence, which proved to be the case in this fight.
